##### Conférence Africaine de l'Internationale

	random = no
	country = SAF
	style = 2
	picture = "Rapallo_conference"

	trigger = { 
		flag = AFR_CONFERENCE_2
		event = 777055
                exists = CON
		OR = {
		war = { country = CON country = ANG }
		war = { country = CON country = MOZ }
		war = { country = CON country = U05 }
		war = { country = CON country = U03 }
		war = { country = VIC country = U04 }
		war = { country = VIC country = U29 }
		war = { country = VIC country = GUI }
		} 
		NOT = {
                government = { type = communist country = CON }
		government = communist
		alliance = { country = CON country = SAF }
		alliance = { country = CON country = GER }
		alliance = { country = SAF country = GER }
		alliance = { country = SAF country = CAN }
		alliance = { country = SAF country = VIC }
                alliance = { country = SAF country = FRA }
		war = { country = SAF country = CON }
		ispuppet = CON
		ispuppet = SAF
		}
		}

	name = "EVT_777257_NAME"

### SAF, when allied to SOMEONE, seizes Namibia

event = {
	id = 777264
	random = no
	country = SAF
	style = 2
	picture = "namibia"

	trigger = { 
		flag = AFR_CONFERENCE_2
                owned = { province = 884 data = CON }
                control = { province = 884 data = CON } 
		OR = {
		war = { country = CON country = ANG }
		war = { country = CON country = MOZ }
		war = { country = CON country = U05 }
		} 
		OR = {
		alliance = { country = SAF country = GER }
		alliance = { country = SAF country = CAN }
		alliance = { country = SAF country = VIC }
		alliance = { country = SAF country = FRA }
		}
		NOT = {
		alliance = { country = CON country = SAF }
		alliance = { country = CON country = GER }
		war = { country = SAF country = CON }
		ispuppet = SAF
		ispuppet = CON
                exists = NAM
		}
		}

	name = "EVT_777264_NAME"
	desc = "EVT_777264_DESC"

	date = { day = 1 month = january year = 1939 }
	offset = 20
